<p>一些人可能會根據所認知到的特徵（比如外貌、衣着、声音、与其他人的相处表現、行为方式）去推定某人的性取向。在社交场合當中嘗試透過外在判斷別人性取向的舉動可稱為<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%8C%E5%BF%97%E9%9B%B7%E8%BE%BE" title="同志雷达">同志雷达</a>——一些研究发现，與碰運气相比，以脸部照片为依據的猜测有着較高的準確度<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-121"><a href="#cite_note-121">[121]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-122"><a href="#cite_note-122">[122]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-123"><a href="#cite_note-123">[123]</a></sup>。2015年的研究表明，同志雷达只是利用<a href="/wiki/LGBT%E5%88%BB%E6%9D%BF%E5%8D%B0%E8%B1%A1" title="LGBT刻板印象">LGBT刻板印象</a>去推測別人性取向的同義詞，而臉型本身並不能準確反映人的性取向<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cox_et_al._(2015)_124-0"><a href="#cite_note-Cox_et_al._(2015)-124">[124]</a></sup>。
</p><p>對別人性取向的推定可能會影響該人所受的待遇。比如，FBI在2004年表示，美國有15.6%向警方落案的<a href="/wiki/%E4%BB%87%E6%81%A8%E7%8A%AF%E7%BD%AA" title="仇恨犯罪">仇恨犯罪</a>「因性取向偏見而起」<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FBI_crime_125-0"><a href="#cite_note-FBI_crime-125">[125]</a></sup>。英國在實施了《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Employment Equality (Sexual Orientation) Regulations 2003" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="2003年就業平等（性取向）条例"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=2003%E5%B9%B4%E5%B0%B1%E6%A5%AD%E5%B9%B3%E7%AD%89%EF%BC%88%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91%EF%BC%89%E6%9D%A1%E4%BE%8B&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="2003年就業平等（性取向）条例（页面不存在）">2003年就業平等（性取向）条例</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Employment_Equality_(Sexual_Orientation)_Regulations_2003" title="en:Employment Equality (Sexual Orientation) Regulations 2003"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Employment Equality (Sexual Orientation) Regulations 2003</span></a></span>）</span></span>》之後<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126"><a href="#cite_note-126">[126]</a></sup>，「不得因为工作者或求职者的性取向、所推定的性取向，或因为他们与某一特定性取向的人有联系，而给予他们较差的待遇」<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127"><a href="#cite_note-127">[127]</a></sup>
</p><p>在欧美文化中，传统规范、价值观、法律皆對異性戀有利<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128"><a href="#cite_note-128">[128]</a></sup>——這包括婚姻和家庭结构<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Garnets,_L._2003_114-1"><a href="#cite_note-Garnets,_L._2003-114">[114]</a></sup>。當地不少人正嘗試改變社會對LGBT人士的偏見，並通過立法保障他們受到平等待遇<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Santaemilia,_J._2008_pp._181–98_119-3"><a href="#cite_note-Santaemilia,_J._2008_pp._181–98-119">[119]</a></sup>。
</p><p>此外亦有不承認同性戀/異性戀/雙性戀區別的文化。它們常以性角色（主動/被動；插入/接受）來把人劃分。在這種劃分底下，「被动」通常与女性气质或自卑有关；「主動」則常跟男性气质或优越有关<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Santaemilia,_J._2008_pp._181–98_119-4"><a href="#cite_note-Santaemilia,_J._2008_pp._181–98-119">[119]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129"><a href="#cite_note-129">[129]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cardoso,_F.L._2005_130-0"><a href="#cite_note-Cardoso,_F.L._2005-130">[130]</a></sup>。 例如，对巴西一个小渔村的调查显示，當地會把男性在性上分為三類——只与男性发生性关系的男性（始终处于被动地位）、只與女性发生性关系的男性、與男女皆發生性關係的男性（始终处于主动地位）。雖然當地人認為扮演被動角色的男性應與另外的那些分類區分開來，但只與女性发生性关系的男性和與男女皆發生性關係的男性則不會作任何區分<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cardoso,_F.L._2005_130-1"><a href="#cite_note-Cardoso,_F.L._2005-130">[130]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.A8.AE.E6.97.8F.E6.AD.A7.E8.A6.96.E8.88.87.E6.94.AF.E6.8F.B4.E7.A8.AE.E6.97.8F.E5.B0.91.E6.95.B8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="種族歧視與支援種族少數">種族歧視與支援種族少數</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="编辑章节：種族歧視與支援種族少數">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>在美国，非高加索人的LGBT人士可能會察覺自己為雙重小眾——他們既不被以高加索人為主的LGBT社群完全了解或接納，亦不被自己的族群所接受<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131"><a href="#cite_note-131">[131]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Masequesmay,_G._2003_132-0"><a href="#cite_note-Masequesmay,_G._2003-132">[132]</a></sup>。很多曾處於主流LGBT社群的非高加索人，要面對因種族與性別雙重刻板印象結合而構成的歧視，比如亞裔美國LGBT人士於很多時候會被當作較為被動和女性化，而非裔美國LGBT人士則被當作較男性化，較具侵略性<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Garnets,_L._2003_114-2"><a href="#cite_note-Garnets,_L._2003-114">[114]</a></sup>。美国有着不少專为特定文化而設的LGBT支援网络，專為越南裔美国酷兒女性而設的「Ô-Môi」便是一例<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Masequesmay,_G._2003_132-1"><a href="#cite_note-Masequesmay,_G._2003-132">[132]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.AE.97.E6.95.99"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="宗教">宗教</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="编辑章节：宗教">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AE%97%E6%95%99%E5%92%8C%E5%90%8C%E6%80%A7%E6%81%8B" title="宗教和同性恋">宗教和同性恋</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%90%8C%E6%80%A7%E6%81%8B%E5%92%8C%E7%8A%B9%E5%A4%AA%E6%95%99" title="同性恋和犹太教">同性恋和犹太教</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%90%8C%E6%80%A7%E6%81%8B%E5%92%8C%E5%9F%BA%E7%9D%A3%E6%95%99" title="同性恋和基督教">同性恋和基督教</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%90%8C%E6%80%A7%E6%81%8B%E5%92%8C%E4%BC%8A%E6%96%AF%E5%85%B0%E6%95%99" title="同性恋和伊斯兰教">同性恋和伊斯兰教</a>、<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%90%8C%E6%80%A7%E6%81%8B%E5%92%8C%E5%8D%B0%E5%BA%A6%E6%95%99&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="同性恋和印度教（页面不存在）">同性恋和印度教</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%90%8C%E6%80%A7%E6%81%8B%E5%92%8C%E4%BD%9B%E6%95%99" title="同性恋和佛教">同性恋和佛教</a></div>
<p>性意識（Sexuality）在宗教的範疇時常是一個具有爭議性的話題，尤其在涉及「性傾向」的這方面。在過去，有些宗教，例如<a href="/wiki/%E5%9F%BA%E7%9D%A3%E6%95%99" title="基督教">基督教</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BC%8A%E6%96%AF%E8%98%AD%E6%95%99" title="伊斯蘭教">伊斯蘭教</a>，對非男女性行為的「同性性行為」採取負面觀點，並有處罰同性<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A6%AA%E5%AF%86%E9%97%9C%E4%BF%82" title="親密關係">親密關係</a>的宗教規範，和對其<a href="/wiki/%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3" title="迫害">迫害</a>的歷史紀錄<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133"><a href="#cite_note-133">[133]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134"><a href="#cite_note-134">[134]</a></sup>。
</p><p>在現代，隨著<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%B8" title="科學">科學</a>知識的進步和對性傾向的了解，有越來越多的宗教和教派，對<a href="/wiki/%E9%9D%9E%E7%95%B0%E6%80%A7%E6%88%80" title="非異性戀">非異性戀</a>者採取接納和寬容的觀點，接受非異性戀性傾向和宗教身份可相互兼容的詮釋<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-135"><a href="#cite_note-135">[135]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136"><a href="#cite_note-136">[136]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137"><a href="#cite_note-137">[137]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138"><a href="#cite_note-138">[138]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139"><a href="#cite_note-139">[139]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140"><a href="#cite_note-140">[140]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.BA.92.E8.81.AF.E7.B6.B2.E8.88.87.E5.AA.92.E9.AB.94"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="互聯網與媒體">互聯網與媒體</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="编辑章节：互聯網與媒體">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>互聯網會在兩方面影響性取向：其能提供一個載體來讓人們產生有關性取向和性認同的話語，繼而促成民間的性觀念<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Santaemilia,_J._2008_pp._181–98_119-5"><a href="#cite_note-Santaemilia,_J._2008_pp._181–98-119">[119]</a></sup>；它允許人們以匿名方式尋找性伴侶，促進人與人之間的交流和聯繫<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141"><a href="#cite_note-141">[141]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E4.BA.BA.E5.8F.A3.E7.B5.B1.E8.A8.88"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="人口統計">人口統計</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="编辑章节：人口統計">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E6%80%A7%E5%82%BE%E5%90%91%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%A3%E7%B5%B1%E8%A8%88" title="性傾向人口統計">性傾向人口統計</a></div>
<p>當代科學調查顯示，不論文化背景如何，社會上大多數人都是異性戀者<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bailey_17-5"><a href="#cite_note-Bailey-17">[17]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LeVay_18-2"><a href="#cite_note-LeVay-18">[18]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:8</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Balthazart_19-2"><a href="#cite_note-Balthazart-19">[19]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:9-10</sup>。雙性戀者則可能認為某種性別相對較有吸引力<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bailey_17-6"><a href="#cite_note-Bailey-17">[17]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LeVay_18-3"><a href="#cite_note-LeVay-18">[18]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:8-9</sup>。與認為兩性有着同等吸引力相比，較多男性為絕對的同性戀者。女性則反之<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bailey_17-7"><a href="#cite_note-Bailey-17">[17]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LeVay_18-4"><a href="#cite_note-LeVay-18">[18]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:8-9</sup>。
</p><p>一糸列以西方文化為背景的研究顯示，平均而言，大約93%的男性和87%的女性自認為絕對的異性戀者，10%的女性及4%的男性自認「偏向於異性戀者」, 1%的女性及0.5%的男性自認為雙性戀者，0.4%的女性及0.5%的男性自認「偏向於同性戀者」，2%的男性和0.5%的女性自認為絕對的同性戀者<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bailey_17-8"><a href="#cite_note-Bailey-17">[17]</a></sup>。一項以67份研究為基礎的分析發現，男男性行為（不論性取向）的終生盛行率為3-5%（東亞）、6-12%（东南亚與南亚）、6-15%（东欧）、6-20%（拉丁美洲）<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142"><a href="#cite_note-142">[142]</a></sup>。国际艾滋病联盟估計，全球有3-16%的<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B7%E7%94%B7%E6%80%A7%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E8%80%85" title="男男性行为者">男男性行为者</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-International_HIV/AIDS_Alliance_2003_143-0"><a href="#cite_note-International_HIV/AIDS_Alliance_2003-143">[143]</a></sup>。
</p><p>同性戀或雙性戀的相對人口比例因調查方法和選擇標準而異。一項於1998年推出的報告表示，根據統計結果，美國有2.8-9%的男性、1-5%的女性為同性戀者或雙性戀者<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144"><a href="#cite_note-144">[144]</a></sup>。
</p><p>一少部分人認為任何人皆沒有性吸引力（<a href="/wiki/%E7%84%A1%E6%80%A7%E6%88%80" title="無性戀">無性戀</a>）。一項2004年的研究顯示，約1%的人口為無性戀者<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bogaert2006_145-0"><a href="#cite_note-Bogaert2006-145">[145]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cnn_146-0"><a href="#cite_note-cnn-146">[146]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E9.87.91.E8.B3.BD.E7.9A.84.E6.95.B8.E6.93.9A"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="金賽的數據">金賽的數據</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="编辑章节：金賽的數據">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E5%B0%94%E5%BC%97%E9%9B%B7%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E9%87%91%E8%B5%9B" title="阿尔弗雷德·金赛">阿尔弗雷德·金赛</a>等人在擇寫《金賽報告》的過程當中，要求研究樣本在<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%91%E8%B3%BD%E9%87%8F%E8%A1%A8" title="金賽量表">量表</a>上為自己的性取向評分。根據金赛等人的數據，很多人為某程度上的雙性戀者，即他們認為兩性都有某種程度的吸引力，不過大多仍偏向於某一種性別。金賽在收集數據時所用到的方法常為人詬病，比如他的人口樣本欠隨機性，包含過多監獄囚犯、男妓、自願參與禁忌性話題的人。不過<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%87%91%E8%B3%BD%E7%A0%94%E7%A9%B6%E6%89%80" title="金賽研究所">金賽研究所</a>的繼任主任保羅·格布哈特在去除有關數據後，得出结论，指出金賽的原始估計沒有顯著受到樣本問題影響<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MDOG_147-0"><a href="#cite_note-MDOG-147">[147]</a></sup>。後世很多研究者認為，金賽因抽样方法存有缺陷，而高估了受到同性性吸引的實際數字<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bailey_17-9"><a href="#cite_note-Bailey-17">[17]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Balthazart_19-3"><a href="#cite_note-Balthazart-19">[19]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:9</sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Lehmiller_148-0"><a href="#cite_note-Lehmiller-148">[148]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:147</sup>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.A4.BE.E6.9C.83.E5.BB.BA.E6.A7.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="社會建構">社會建構</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="编辑章节：社會建構">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">参见：<a href="/wiki/%E9%85%B7%E5%84%BF%E7%90%86%E8%AE%BA" title="酷儿理论">酷儿理论</a></div>
<p>由於性傾向的複雜和多面向成份，所以一些研究者主張那是由歷史和<a href="/wiki/%E7%A4%BE%E4%BC%9A%E5%BB%BA%E6%9E%84%E4%B8%BB%E4%B9%89" title="社会建构主义">社會建構</a>下所誕生的產物，此一主張尤見於<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%85%B7%E5%85%92%E7%90%86%E8%AB%96" title="酷兒理論">酷兒理論</a>的研究者。1976年，歷史學家兼哲學家<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B1%B3%E6%AD%87%E7%88%BE%C2%B7%E7%A6%8F%E6%9F%AF" title="米歇爾·福柯">米歇爾·福柯</a>在《<a href="/wiki/%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%B2_(%E7%A6%8F%E6%9F%AF%E8%91%97)" title="性史 (福柯著)">性史</a>》中提出，同性戀的概念在18世紀時並不存在，人們的認識對象只有「sodomy」（雞姦）這種性行為，而那在當時是一種常被忽視但會被嚴厲懲罰的刑事罪行。他指出「性（Sexuality）是一種因為工業革命和資本主義而產生的現代概念」<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup>。另有学者认为，古今同性戀之間有着明显的连续性<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Norton_2016_150-0"><a href="#cite_note-Norton_2016-150">[150]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Boswell_1989_17–36_151-0"><a href="#cite_note-Boswell_1989_17–36-151">[151]</a></sup>。科學哲學家<a href="/wiki/%E8%BF%88%E5%85%8B%E5%B0%94%C2%B7%E9%B2%81%E6%96%AF" title="迈克尔·鲁斯">迈克尔·鲁斯</a>表示，受福柯影响的建构主义方法主要以經過片面讀取的歷史記錄為依據，它們會把同性戀者的存在跟人們標籖或對待他們的方式混為一談<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup>。
</p><p>在現今大多數社會，人們的性認同主要以其伴侶的性別為依據。但在一些社會當中，人們會把性角色（插入方還是受方）當作主要依據，並以之來定義性本身<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WHOMSM_153-0"><a href="#cite_note-WHOMSM-153">[153]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup>。在西方文化中，人们有意义地談論LGB認同或社群。但在一些文化中，同性恋和异性恋的标签并不强调社會認同，或建基於性取向的社群歸屬<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.83.E8.A6.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="參見">參見</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="编辑章节：參見">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span id=".E5.8F.83.E8.80.83.E6.96.87.E7.8D.BB"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="參考文獻">參考文獻</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="编辑章节：參考文獻">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<li id="cite_note-AmPsycholAssn-definitions-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-AmPsycholAssn-definitions_3-0"><sup><b>3.0</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-AmPsycholAssn-definitions_3-1"><sup><b>3.1</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-AmPsycholAssn-definitions_3-2"><sup><b>3.2</b></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web"><a class="external text" href="https://www.apa.org/pi/lgbt/resources/sexuality-definitions.pdf" rel="nofollow">Definitions Related to Sexual Orientation and Gender Diversity in APA Documents</a> <span style="font-size:85%;">(PDF)</span>. <a href="/wiki/%E7%BE%8E%E5%9B%BD%E5%BF%83%E7%90%86%E5%AD%A6%E4%BC%9A" title="美国心理学会">American Psychological Association</a>: 6. 2015 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2020-02-06</span>]</span>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20210122054116/https://www.apa.org/pi/lgbt/resources/sexuality-definitions.pdf" rel="nofollow">存档</a> <span style="font-size:85%;">(PDF)</span>于2021-01-22）. <q>Sexual orientation refers to the sex of those to whom one is sexually and romantically attracted. [...] [It is] one's enduring sexual attraction to male partners, female partners, or both. Sexual orientation may be heterosexual, samesex (gay or lesbian), or bisexual. [...] A person may be attracted to men, women, both, neither, or to people who are genderqueer, androgynous, or have other gender identities. Individuals may identify as lesbian, gay, heterosexual, bisexual, queer, pansexual, or asexual, among others. [...] Categories of sexual orientation typically have included attraction to members of one's own sex (gay men or lesbians), attraction to members of the other sex (heterosexuals), and attraction to members of both sexes (bisexuals). While these categories continue to be widely used, research has suggested that sexual orientation does not always appear in such definable categories and instead occurs on a continuum [...]. Some people identify as pansexual or queer in terms of their sexual orientation, which means they define their sexual orientation outside of the gender binary of 'male' and 'female' only.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;rft.btitle=Definitions+Related+to+Sexual+Orientation+and+Gender+Diversity+in+APA+Documents&amp;rft.date=2015&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.pages=6&amp;rft.pub=American+Psychological+Association&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.apa.org%2Fpi%2Flgbt%2Fresources%2Fsexuality-definitions.pdf&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

Cengage Learning. 2014: 82 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2016-02-11</span>]</span>. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/978-1-305-17689-8" title="Special:网络书源/978-1-305-17689-8"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 978-1-305-17689-8</a>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20161130141623/https://books.google.com/books?id=fofaAgAAQBAJ&amp;pg=PA82" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2016-11-30）. <q>The reason some individuals develop a gay sexual identity has not been definitively established  – nor do we yet understand the development of heterosexuality. The American Psychological Association (APA) takes the position that a variety of factors impact a person's sexuality. The most recent literature from the APA says that sexual orientation is not a choice that can be changed at will, and that sexual orientation is most likely the result of a complex interaction of environmental, cognitive and biological factors...is shaped at an early age...[and evidence suggests] biological, including genetic or inborn hormonal factors, play a significant role in a person's sexuality (American Psychological Association 2010).</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;rft.au=Riedmann%2C+Agnes&amp;rft.au=Stewart%2C+Susan+D&amp;rft.aufirst=Mary+Ann&amp;rft.aulast=Lamanna&amp;rft.btitle=Marriages%2C+Families%2C+and+Relationships%3A+Making+Choices+in+a+Diverse+Society&amp;rft.date=2014&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=978-1-305-17689-8&amp;rft.pages=82&amp;rft.pub=Cengage+Learning&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DfofaAgAAQBAJ%26pg%3DPA82&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Stuart-16"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-Stuart_16-0"><sup><b>16.0</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-Stuart_16-1"><sup><b>16.1</b></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Gail Wiscarz Stuart. <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=ivALBAAAQBAJ&amp;pg=PA502" rel="nofollow">Principles and Practice of Psychiatric Nursing</a>. <a href="/wiki/%E6%84%9B%E6%80%9D%E5%94%AF%E7%88%BE" title="愛思唯爾">Elsevier Health Sciences</a>. 2014: 502 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2016-02-11</span>]</span>. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/978-0-323-29412-6" title="Special:网络书源/978-0-323-29412-6"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 978-0-323-29412-6</a>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20161130185850/https://books.google.com/books?id=ivALBAAAQBAJ&amp;pg=PA502" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2016-11-30）. <q>No conclusive evidence supports any one specific cause of homosexuality; however, most researchers agree that biological and social factors influence the development of sexual orientation.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;rft.au=Gail+Wiscarz+Stuart&amp;rft.btitle=Principles+and+Practice+of+Psychiatric+Nursing&amp;rft.date=2014&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-323-29412-6&amp;rft.pages=502&amp;rft.pub=Elsevier+Health+Sciences&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DivALBAAAQBAJ%26pg%3DPA502&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>

<li id="cite_note-fluidity-49"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-fluidity_49-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">*<cite class="citation journal">Bailey, J. Michael; Vasey, Paul; Diamond, Lisa; Breedlove, S. Marc; Vilain, Eric; Epprecht, Marc. <a class="external text" href="https://www.researchgate.net/publication/301639075" rel="nofollow">Sexual Orientation, Controversy, and Science</a>. Psychological Science in the Public Interest. 2016, <b>17</b> (2): 45–101 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2021-03-31</span>]</span>. <a class="external text" href="//www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/27113562" rel="nofollow"><span title="公共医学识别码">PMID 27113562</span></a>. <a class="external text" href="https://dx.doi.org/10.1177%2F1529100616637616" rel="nofollow"><span title="數位物件識別號">doi:10.1177/1529100616637616</span></a>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20200414090908/https://www.researchgate.net/publication/301639075_Sexual_Orientation_Controversy_and_Science" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2020-04-14）. <q>Sexual fluidity is situation-dependent flexibility in a person’s sexual responsiveness, which makes it possible for some individuals to experience desires for either men or women under certain circumstances regardless of their overall sexual orientation....We expect that in all cultures the vast majority of individuals are sexually predisposed exclusively to the other sex (i.e., heterosexual) and that only a minority of individuals are sexually predisposed (whether exclusively or non-exclusively) to the same sex.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;rft.atitle=Sexual+Orientation%2C+Controversy%2C+and+Science&amp;rft.au=Breedlove%2C+S.+Marc&amp;rft.au=Diamond%2C+Lisa&amp;rft.au=Epprecht%2C+Marc&amp;rft.au=Vasey%2C+Paul&amp;rft.au=Vilain%2C+Eric&amp;rft.aufirst=J.+Michael&amp;rft.aulast=Bailey&amp;rft.date=2016&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.issue=2&amp;rft.jtitle=Psychological+Science+in+the+Public+Interest&amp;rft.pages=45-101&amp;rft.volume=17&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.researchgate.net%2Fpublication%2F301639075&amp;rft_id=info%3Adoi%2F10.1177%2F1529100616637616&amp;rft_id=info%3Apmid%2F27113562&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span>
<ul><li><cite class="citation book">Dennis Coon; John O. Mitterer. <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=EYwjCQAAQBAJ&amp;pg=PA372" rel="nofollow">Introduction to Psychology: Gateways to Mind and Behavior with Concept Maps and Reviews</a>. Cengage Learning. 2012: 372 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2016-02-18</span>]</span>. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/978-1111833633" title="Special:网络书源/978-1111833633"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 978-1111833633</a>. <q>Sexual orientation is a deep part of personal identity and is usually quite stable. Starting with their earliest erotic feelings, most people remember being attracted to either the opposite sex or the same sex. [...] The fact that sexual orientation is usually quite stable doesn't rule out the possibility that for some people sexual behavior may change during the course of a lifetime.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;rft.au=Dennis+Coon&amp;rft.au=John+O.+Mitterer&amp;rft.btitle=Introduction+to+Psychology%3A+Gateways+to+Mind+and+Behavior+with+Concept+Maps+and+Reviews&amp;rft.date=2012&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=978-1111833633&amp;rft.pages=372&amp;rft.pub=Cengage+Learning&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DEYwjCQAAQBAJ%26pg%3DPA372&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></li>
<li><cite class="citation book">Eric Anderson; Mark McCormack. <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=7_AgDAAAQBAJ&amp;pg=PA47" rel="nofollow">Measuring and Surveying Bisexuality</a>. The Changing Dynamics of Bisexual Men's Lives. <a href="/wiki/%E6%96%BD%E6%99%AE%E6%9E%97%E6%A0%BC%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%2B%E5%95%86%E4%B8%9A%E5%AA%92%E4%BD%93" title="施普林格科学+商业媒体">Springer Science &amp; Business Media</a>. 2016: 47 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2019-06-22</span>]</span>. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/978-3-319-29412-4" title="Special:网络书源/978-3-319-29412-4"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 978-3-319-29412-4</a>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20210824071645/https://books.google.com/books?id=7_AgDAAAQBAJ&amp;pg=PA47" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2021-08-24）. <q>[R]esearch suggests that women's sexual orientation is slightly more likely to change than men's (Baumeister 2000; Kinnish et al. 2005). The notion that sexual orientation can change over time is known as <i>sexual fluidity</i>. Even if sexual fluidity exists for some women, it does not mean that the majority of women will change sexual orientations as they age – rather, sexuality is stable over time for the majority of people.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;rft.atitle=Measuring+and+Surveying+Bisexuality&amp;rft.au=Eric+Anderson&amp;rft.au=Mark+McCormack&amp;rft.btitle=The+Changing+Dynamics+of+Bisexual+Men%27s+Lives&amp;rft.date=2016&amp;rft.genre=bookitem&amp;rft.isbn=978-3-319-29412-4&amp;rft.pages=47&amp;rft.pub=Springer+Science+%26+Business+Media&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3D7_AgDAAAQBAJ%26pg%3DPA47&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></li></ul>
</span></li>

John Wiley &amp; Sons Ltd. 2018 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2021-04-06</span>]</span>. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/9781119164739" title="Special:网络书源/9781119164739"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 9781119164739</a>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20201231045623/https://books.google.com/books?id=JXJGDwAAQBAJ" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2020-12-31）.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;rft.aufirst=Justin&amp;rft.aulast=Lehmiller&amp;rft.btitle=The+Psychology+of+Human+Sexuality&amp;rft.date=2018&amp;rft.edition=Second&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=9781119164739&amp;rft.pub=John+Wiley+%26+Sons+Ltd&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DJXJGDwAAQBAJ&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-149"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-149">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=dMAtGvry_IMC&amp;pg=PA32&amp;lpg=PA32&amp;dq=china+heterosexuality+love+western&amp;source=web&amp;ots=PKv2BfyPpd&amp;sig=s43w6PzlNOgefEsjpHViwrxkM6A&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;oi=book_result&amp;resnum=1&amp;ct=result" rel="nofollow"><i>Chinese Femininities, Chinese Masculinities: A Reader</i></a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20170312212325/https://books.google.com/books?id=dMAtGvry_IMC&amp;pg=PA32&amp;lpg=PA32&amp;dq=china+heterosexuality+love+western&amp;source=web&amp;ots=PKv2BfyPpd&amp;sig=s43w6PzlNOgefEsjpHViwrxkM6A&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;oi=book_result&amp;resnum=1&amp;ct=result" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）, by Susan Brownell &amp; Jeffrey N. Wasserstrom (Univ. of Calif. Press, 2002 (<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r61200749" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E6%A0%87%E5%87%86%E4%B9%A6%E5%8F%B7" title="国际标准书号">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/0-520-22116-8" title="Special:网络书源/0-520-22116-8">0-520-22116-8</a>, <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r61200749" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E6%A0%87%E5%87%86%E4%B9%A6%E5%8F%B7" title="国际标准书号">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/978-0-520-22116-1" title="Special:网络书源/978-0-520-22116-1">978-0-520-22116-1</a>)). Quote: "The problem with sexuality: Some scholars have argued that maleness and femaleness were not closely linked to sexuality in China. Michel Foucault's <i><a href="/wiki/%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%B2_(%E7%A6%8F%E6%9F%AF%E8%91%97)" title="性史 (福柯著)">The History of Sexuality</a></i> (which deals primarily with Western civilization and western Europe) began to influence some China scholars in the 1980s. Foucault's insight was to demonstrate that sexuality has a history; it is not fixed psycho-biological drive that is the same for all humans according to their sex, but rather it is a cultural construct inseparable from gender constructs. After unmooring sexuality from biology, he anchored it in history, arguing that this thing we now call sexuality came into existence in the eighteenth-century West and did not exist previously in this form. "Sexuality" is an invention of the modern state, the industrial revolution, and capitalism. Taking this insight as a starting point, scholars have slowly been compiling the history of sexuality in China. The works by Tani Barlow, discussed above, were also foundational in this trend. Barlow observes that, in the West, heterosexuality is the primary site for the production of gender: a woman truly becomes a woman only in relation to a man's heterosexual desire. By contrast, in China before the 1920s the "jia" (linage unit, family) was the primary site for the production of gender: marriage and sexuality were to serve the lineage by producing the next generation of lineage members; personal love and pleasure were secondary to this goal. Barlow argues that this has two theoretical implications: (1) it is not possible to write a Chinese history of heterosexuality, sexuality as an institution, and sexual identities in the European metaphysical sense, and (2) it is not appropriate to ground discussions of Chinese gender processes in the sexed body so central in "Western" gender processes. Here she echoes Furth's argument that, before the early twentieth century, sex-identity grounded on anatomical difference did not hold a central place in Chinese constructions of gender. And she echoes the point illustrated in detail in Sommer's chapter on male homosexuality in the Qing legal code: a man could engage in homosexual behavior without calling into question his manhood so long as his behavior did not threaten the patriarchal Confucian family structure."</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Norton_2016-150"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Norton_2016_150-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation book">Norton, Rictor. <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=DkTqDAAAQBAJ" rel="nofollow">Myth of the Modern Homosexual</a>. Bloomsbury Academic. 2016 <span class="reference-accessdate"> [<span class="nowrap">2021-04-09</span>]</span>. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/9781474286923" title="Special:网络书源/9781474286923"><span title="国际标准书号">ISBN</span> 9781474286923</a>. （原始内容<a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20210511080439/https://books.google.com/books?id=DkTqDAAAQBAJ" rel="nofollow">存档</a>于2021-05-11）.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fzh.wikipedia.org%3A%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%96%E5%90%91&amp;rft.aufirst=Rictor&amp;rft.aulast=Norton&amp;rft.btitle=Myth+of+the+Modern+Homosexual&amp;rft.date=2016&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.isbn=9781474286923&amp;rft.pub=Bloomsbury+Academic&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DDkTqDAAAQBAJ&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span> The author has made adapted and expanded portions of this book available online as <a class="external text" href="http://rictornorton.co.uk/extracts.htm" rel="nofollow"><i>A Critique of Social Constructionism and Postmodern Queer Theory</i></a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20190330132639/http://rictornorton.co.uk/extracts.htm" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）.</span>
